G-Dragon learned Korean classical dance, and his dance has the uniqueness of a combination of hip-hop and Korean classical dance. G-Dragon's dance is distinctly different from the dancers around him. His improvisational moves, which use his entire soles of his feet and raise his foot, give it the vibe of Korean folk dance.
